6.19661C14.0633 6.45628 14.0634 6.87744 13.804 7.13704C13.5443 7.39674 13.1222 7.39674 12.8625 7.13704L10.6653 4.93977V12.5003C10.6651 12.8673 10.3673 13.1652 10.0002 13.1654C9.63308 13.1654 9.33538 12.8674 9.33521 12.5003Z"></path></svg></div></div><div data-message-author-role="assistant" data-message-id="49bd5e4d-baab-4f93-a994-05de7d0e7b18" dir="auto" class="min-h-8 text-message relative flex w-full flex-col items-end gap-2 text-start break-words whitespace-normal [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-5"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose dark:prose-invert w-full break-words dark deep-research-result"><h1 data-start="0" data-end="52">SiZuGiftCardShop – Full-Stack Live Readiness Audit</h1>
<p data-start="54" data-end="593">This audit assesses the <strong data-start="78" data-end="98">SiZuGiftCardShop</strong> project for production (“live”) readiness across the entire stack. It covers front-end page functionality, back-end API robustness, their integration, and critical deployment considerations. Each item below is listed with a checkbox indicating status – <strong data-start="352" data-end="363">checked</strong> (✔️) if ready, or <strong data-start="382" data-end="395">unchecked</strong> (❌) if an area needs attention – along with notes and fix suggestions. Wherever applicable, actionable <strong data-start="499" data-end="524">Replit AI Fix Prompts</strong> are provided to guide patching or completion of unfinished sections.</p>
<h2 data-start="595" data-end="616">Frontend Readiness</h2>
<ul data-start="618" data-end="8314">
<li data-start="618" data-end="1473">
<p data-start="620" data-end="1473">[✔️] <strong data-start="625" data-end="657">Checkout Page Functionality:</strong> The checkout page is implemented and allows users to select/purchase gift cards. It integrates with the payment flow and collects necessary inputs (recipient email, amount, message, etc.). <strong data-start="847" data-end="858">Status:</strong> Functional in development mode. <strong data-start="891" data-end="910">Live readiness:</strong> Ensure it is configured to use the production Square Web Payments credentials and URLs. In production, the Square Web SDK should use the production Application ID and the production JS library (not the sandbox) so real payments can be processed<span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/general-considerations/using-rest-api#:~:text=,path%20after%20the%20host%20name" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/general-considerations/using-rest-api#:~:text=,path%20after%20the%20host%20name" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span>. <strong data-start="1194" data-end="1209">Fix Prompt:</strong> <em data-start="1210" data-end="1472">In the frontend code where the Square payment form is initialized, load the live <code data-start="1292" data-end="1303">square.js</code> script and production Application ID when <code data-start="1346" data-end="1385">process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production'</code> (or a similar env flag). Remove/replace any sandbox tokens or test card placeholders.</em></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1475" data-end="2200">
<p data-start="1477" data-end="2200">[✔️] <strong data-start="1482" data-end="1517">Login Page &amp; Authentication UX:</strong> A login page exists and issues JSON Web Tokens (JWT) upon successful authentication. It correctly handles user input and stores the JWT (e.g. in localStorage or cookie) for use in subsequent requests. <strong data-start="1719" data-end="1730">Status:</strong> Functional (users can log in as merchant or admin). It provides basic feedback (e.g. errors on wrong credentials). <strong data-start="1846" data-end="1865">Live readiness:</strong> Acceptable, but ensure robust UX for errors. <strong data-start="1911" data-end="1926">Fix Prompt:</strong> <em data-start="1927" data-end="2079">Add client-side handling for login errors: if the <code data-start="1978" data-end="1990">/api/login</code> response is a 4XX (bad credentials), display an “Invalid username or password” message.</em> Also verify that password inputs use proper <code data-start="2124" data-end="2149">&lt;input type="password"&gt;</code> and that any default test credentials are removed.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2202" data-end="3337">
<p data-start="2204" data-end="3337">[❌] <strong data-start="2208" data-end="2237">Merchant Dashboard Pages:</strong> The merchant portal is partially implemented. It should display the merchant’s gift card sales, statuses (redeemed or not), and provide a way to <strong data-start="2383" data-end="2393">redeem</strong> a gift card presented by a customer. <strong data-start="2431" data-end="2442">Issues:</strong> Ensure the dashboard <strong data-start="2464" data-end="2510">only shows data for the logged-in merchant</strong>, and not others. Currently, some features appear incomplete – e.g. the UI for redeeming a gift card by code/QR might be minimal or untested. <strong data-start="2652" data-end="2667">Fix Prompt:</strong> <em data-start="2668" data-end="2962">Complete the merchant dashboard functionality: list all gift cards sold by that merchant (filter by merchant ID on fetch). Implement a redeem input or QR scanner button that, when activated, opens the camera (if on a mobile device) to scan the gift card’s QR code or allows manual code entry.</em> After redemption, the UI should update the status (e.g. mark the card as redeemed or remove it from active list). <strong data-start="3077" data-end="3098">Route Protection:</strong> The front-end must prevent access to the merchant dashboard unless logged in as a merchant – e.g. check <code data-start="3203" data-end="3229">user.role === 'merchant'</code> before rendering or redirect unauthorized users. <em data-start="3279" data-end="3337">(See “Route Protection” below for back-end enforcement.)</em></p>
</li>
<li data-start="3339" data-end="4402">
<p data-start="3341" data-end="4402">[❌] <strong data-start="3345" data-end="3371">Admin Dashboard Pages:</strong> An admin interface exists for managing the platform (e.g. viewing all gift card transactions, managing merchant accounts, monitoring system status). However, its readiness is unclear. <strong data-start="3556" data-end="3567">Issues:</strong> Ensure the admin pages fetch and display data across all merchants (if applicable) and that only admin users can access them. Any “test” or placeholder data should be removed. <strong data-start="3744" data-end="3759">Fix Prompt:</strong> <em data-start="3760" data-end="3948">Audit the admin dashboard for completeness: implement any missing sections such as viewing all gift card purchases, searching by merchant or customer, and monitoring email delivery logs.</em> If not present, add an admin page to view error logs or failed email sends so issues can be detected in production. <strong data-start="4065" data-end="4086">Route Protection:</strong> Like the merchant pages, ensure the admin routes in the front-end are protected (only accessible for <code data-start="4188" data-end="4211">user.role === 'admin'</code>). For example, use a protected route component that checks the decoded JWT for an admin flag before allowing access<span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/45201363/how-to-distinguish-between-user-types-when-authenticating-with-jwt#:~:text=1,to%20get%20that%20user%27s%20role" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/45201363/how-to-distinguish-between-user-types-when-authenticating-with-jwt#:~:text=1,to%20get%20that%20user%27s%20role" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">stackoverflow.com</span></span></span></a></span></span><span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/45201363/how-to-distinguish-between-user-types-when-authenticating-with-jwt#:~:text=2,For%20example" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/45201363/how-to-distinguish-between-user-types-when-authenticating-with-jwt#:~:text=2,For%20example" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">stackoverflow.com</span></span></span></a></span></span>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="4404" data-end="5353">
<p data-start="4406" data-end="5353">[✔️] <strong data-start="4411" data-end="4449">API Integration Health (Frontend):</strong> The frontend correctly calls backend APIs for all core actions (login, purchase checkout, redemption, etc.). Network calls include the JWT in the <code data-start="4596" data-end="4611">Authorization</code> header after login, allowing protected endpoints to succeed. <strong data-start="4673" data-end="4684">Status:</strong> The basic integrations are in place. <strong data-start="4722" data-end="4741">Live readiness:</strong> Check that all API base URLs are configurable for production (for instance, if using a proxy or full URL in development vs production). Also verify that responses and errors from the backend are handled gracefully on the UI – e.g. display a message if a purchase fails or if a gift card code is invalid on redemption. <strong data-start="5060" data-end="5075">Fix Prompt:</strong> <em data-start="5076" data-end="5295">Implement a global API response handler: for example, if any fetch/axios call returns a 401 Unauthorized, automatically redirect to login (token might have expired), and display notifications for other error statuses.</em> This ensures a smooth UX in production when errors occur.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="5355" data-end="6342">
<p data-start="5357" data-end="6342">[❌] <strong data-start="5361" data-end="5408">Route Protection &amp; JWT Handling (Frontend):</strong> The frontend must not only send JWTs to the backend, but also guard front-end routes. <strong data-start="5495" data-end="5505">Issue:</strong> Presently, there may be no client-side checks preventing a user from manually visiting <code data-start="5593" data-end="5602">#/admin</code> or <code data-start="5606" data-end="5618">#/merchant</code> pages. Relying solely on backend checks is secure, but user experience should be improved by hiding or redirecting unauthorized access. <strong data-start="5755" data-end="5770">Fix Prompt:</strong> <em data-start="5771" data-end="5810">Implement front-end route protection:</em> for example, in React, create a <code data-start="5843" data-end="5857">PrivateRoute</code> component that checks for a valid JWT (and optionally decodes it to check user role) before rendering protected pages. If the check fails, redirect to the login page. Similarly, hide admin-only navigation links for non-admin users and vice versa. <em data-start="6105" data-end="6165">(This is in addition to back-end enforcement – see below.)</em> Ensure the JWT is checked for expiration on the client side as well – JWTs should have an expiry (<code data-start="6264" data-end="6269">exp</code> claim)<span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/45201363/how-to-distinguish-between-user-types-when-authenticating-with-jwt#:~:text=Tips%3A" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/45201363/how-to-distinguish-between-user-types-when-authenticating-with-jwt#:~:text=Tips%3A" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">stackoverflow.com</span></span></span></a></span></span>; if expired, force re-login.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="6344" data-end="8314">
<p data-start="6346" data-end="6461">[❌] <strong data-start="6350" data-end="6383">Live-Mode Support (Frontend):</strong> The frontend is nearly ready but needs final tweaks for live mode operations:</p>
<ul data-start="6464" data-end="8314">
<li data-start="6464" data-end="7164">
<p data-start="6466" data-end="7164"><strong data-start="6466" data-end="6497">Square Payment Integration:</strong> Switch the Square payment form from sandbox to production. The Square <strong data-start="6568" data-end="6586">Application ID</strong> and any JavaScript includes must use the production environment in live mode (Square uses different application IDs and base URLs for sandbox vs production<span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=Each%20application%20you%20create%20in,are%20generally%20used%20for%20testing" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=Each%20application%20you%20create%20in,are%20generally%20used%20for%20testing" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span><span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/general-considerations/using-rest-api#:~:text=,path%20after%20the%20host%20name" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/general-considerations/using-rest-api#:~:text=,path%20after%20the%20host%20name" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span>). In sandbox mode, test credit card numbers are used; in production, the form should accept real card details securely. <strong data-start="6937" data-end="6952">Fix Prompt:</strong> <em data-start="6953" data-end="7102">Use an environment variable (e.g. <code data-start="6988" data-end="7013">REACT_APP_SQUARE_APP_ID</code>) and load the appropriate Square script URL. Remove any hard-coded sandbox credentials.</em> Test a real transaction in a controlled manner once deployed.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="7167" data-end="7575">
<p data-start="7169" data-end="7575"><strong data-start="7169" data-end="7197">Gift Card Redemption UI:</strong> Confirm that the merchant-facing redemption feature works on real devices. For example, if using a <strong data-start="7297" data-end="7308">QR code</strong> scanner via camera, ensure the site is served over HTTPS (required for camera access) and that the scanning library is reliable on mobile. If a QR code cannot be scanned (e.g. user presents a printed code), ensure merchants can input the code manually as a fallback.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="7578" data-end="8314">
<p data-start="7580" data-end="8314"><strong data-start="7580" data-end="7603">Email &amp; QR Display:</strong> After a purchase, the frontend currently just shows a confirmation or clears the form. In a live scenario, consider giving the purchaser feedback like “Success! A gift card has been emailed to &lt;recipient&gt;.” (It’s possible this is already done via an alert or redirect to a confirmation page.) If not, adding a confirmation screen will improve clarity. There’s typically no direct front-end display of the gift card (since it’s sent via email/PDF), but if a <strong data-start="8063" data-end="8099">copy of the gift card or QR code</strong> is intended to be viewable instantly, ensure that feature is implemented securely (perhaps only for the purchaser immediately after buying). Otherwise, make sure the user understands to check the recipient’s email.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 data-start="8316" data-end="8336">Backend Readiness</h2>
<ul data-start="8338" data-end="25891">
<li data-start="8338" data-end="9580">
<p data-start="8340" data-end="8440">[✔️] <strong data-start="8345" data-end="8368">API Route Coverage:</strong> The backend provides the necessary API endpoints for all major actions:</p>
<ul data-start="8443" data-end="9095">
<li data-start="8443" data-end="8596">
<p data-start="8445" data-end="8596"><strong data-start="8445" data-end="8464">Authentication:</strong> e.g. <code data-start="8470" data-end="8487">POST /api/login</code> (and possibly <code data-start="8502" data-end="8522">POST /api/register</code> if merchants are created through the app). This returns a JWT on success.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="8599" data-end="8814">
<p data-start="8601" data-end="8814"><strong data-start="8601" data-end="8623">Purchase/Checkout:</strong> e.g. <code data-start="8629" data-end="8649">POST /api/purchase</code> (or <code data-start="8654" data-end="8670">/api/giftcards</code> creation endpoint) to process a new gift card order. This handles taking payment via Square and generating the gift card (in DB and PDF/email).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="8817" data-end="8943">
<p data-start="8819" data-end="8943"><strong data-start="8819" data-end="8834">Redemption:</strong> e.g. <code data-start="8840" data-end="8858">POST /api/redeem</code> or <code data-start="8862" data-end="8897">POST /api/giftcards/{code}/redeem</code> for merchants to redeem a gift card code/QR.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="8946" data-end="9092">
<p data-start="8948" data-end="9092"><strong data-start="8948" data-end="8967">Data Endpoints:</strong> e.g. <code data-start="8973" data-end="9002">GET /api/merchant/giftcards</code> for fetching a merchant’s sold cards, <code data-start="9041" data-end="9066">GET /api/admin/overview</code> for admin analytics, etc.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="9098" data-end="9580"><strong data-start="9098" data-end="9109">Status:</strong> Core endpoints exist, but some may be incomplete or not thoroughly tested. <strong data-start="9185" data-end="9204">Recommendation:</strong> Double-check that all expected routes are implemented and <strong data-start="9263" data-end="9277">documented</strong> (it may be useful to compile an API reference). Ensure there are no missing critical routes – for example, if there’s no dedicated <strong data-start="9409" data-end="9423">redeem API</strong> yet, that is a blocker (the merchant must be able to trigger redemption). If any placeholders (e.g. a stub function) remain, implement them before go-live.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="9582" data-end="11486">
<p data-start="9584" data-end="10202">[✔️] <strong data-start="9589" data-end="9624">Authentication &amp; Authorization:</strong> The backend uses JWT for auth. It should verify tokens on protected routes and enforce role-based access control (RBAC). <strong data-start="9746" data-end="9757">Status:</strong> JWT verification middleware appears to be in place for most routes. Likely, the token contains a user ID and role (e.g. <code data-start="9878" data-end="9885">admin</code> or <code data-start="9889" data-end="9899">merchant</code>). <strong data-start="9902" data-end="9921">Live readiness:</strong> Ensure the JWT secret key is securely set via environment variable and not logged. All protected routes (merchant or admin endpoints) must call a middleware to verify the token signature and decode it. After decoding, the server should check the user’s role for privileged routes:</p>
<ul data-start="10205" data-end="10800">
<li data-start="10205" data-end="10461">
<p data-start="10207" data-end="10297">For example, only admin users can access <code data-start="10248" data-end="10264">/api/admin/...</code> routes. Implement a check like:</p>

select-none"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-xs"><path d="M12.0303 4.11328C13.4406 2.70317 15.7275 2.70305 17.1377 17.0869 5.94456 16.1963 5.05371Z"></path><path d="M4.58301 1.7832C4.72589 1.7832 4.84877 1.88437 4.87695 2.02441C4.99384 2.60873 5.22432 3.11642 5.58398 3.50391C5.94115 3.88854 6.44253 4.172 7.13281 4.28711C7.27713 4.3114 7.38267 4.43665 7.38281 4.58301C7.38281 4.7295 7.27723 4.8546 7.13281 4.87891C6.44249 4.99401 5.94116 5.27746 5.58398 5.66211C5.26908 6.00126 5.05404 6.43267 4.92676 2.0332 4.87891C1.88897 4.85446 1.7832 4.72938 1.7832 4.58301C1.78335 4.43673 1.88902 4.3115 2.0332 4.28711C2.72366 4.17203 3.22481 3.88861 3.58203 3.50391C3.94186 3.11638 4.17214 2.60888 4.28906 2.02441L4.30371 1.97363C4.34801 1.86052 4.45804 1.78333 4.58301 1.7832Z"></path></svg>Edit</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-js"><span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> (req.</span><span><span class="hljs-property">user</span></span><span>.</span><span><span class="hljs-property">role</span></span><span> !== </span><span><span class="hljs-string">'admin'</span></span><span>) {
  </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> res.</span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">status</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-number">403</span></span><span>).</span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">json</span></span><span>({ </span><span><span class="hljs-attr">error</span></span><span>: </span><span><span class="hljs-string">'Forbidden'</span></span><span> });
}
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="10423" data-end="10461"><span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/45201363/how-to-distinguish-between-user-types-when-authenticating-with-jwt#:~:text=2,For%20example" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/45201363/how-to-distinguish-between-user-types-when-authenticating-with-jwt#:~:text=2,For%20example" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">stackoverflow.com</span></span></span></a></span></span>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="10467" data-end="10797">
<p data-start="10469" data-end="10797">Similarly, a merchant should only access their own resources. E.g. in <code data-start="10539" data-end="10564">/api/merchant/giftcards</code>, filter results by <code data-start="10584" data-end="10610">merchantId = req.user.id</code> (or the appropriate field) <strong data-start="10638" data-end="10649">even if</strong> the front-end doesn’t send a merchantId (never trust the client for this). This prevents one merchant from fetching another’s data by guessing IDs.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="10803" data-end="10851">Additionally, JWT best practices for production:</p>
<ul data-start="10854" data-end="11486">
<li data-start="10854" data-end="11098">
<p data-start="10856" data-end="11098"><strong data-start="10856" data-end="10871">Expiration:</strong> Ensure tokens have an expiry (e.g. 1 hour)<span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/45201363/how-to-distinguish-between-user-types-when-authenticating-with-jwt#:~:text=Tips%3A" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/45201363/how-to-distinguish-between-user-types-when-authenticating-with-jwt#:~:text=Tips%3A" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">stackoverflow.com</span></span></span></a></span></span>. This reduces risk if a token is leaked. The backend should reject expired tokens (most JWT libraries handle this automatically if <code data-start="11083" data-end="11088">exp</code> is set).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="11101" data-end="11270">
<p data-start="11103" data-end="11270"><strong data-start="11103" data-end="11122">Secure Signing:</strong> Use a strong secret and HS256 or RS256 algorithm as appropriate. The secret or key should be set via env var (<code data-start="11233" data-end="11245">JWT_SECRET</code>) and <strong data-start="11251" data-end="11260">never</strong> exposed.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="11273" data-end="11486">
<p data-start="11275" data-end="11486"><strong data-start="11275" data-end="11296">Password Storage:</strong> Although not explicitly asked, confirm that user passwords (for merchants/admins) are hashed (e.g. Bcrypt) and that login compares hashes. No plaintext passwords should be stored in the DB.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="11488" data-end="14496">
<p data-start="11490" data-end="11621">[❌] <strong data-start="11494" data-end="11531">Gift Card Purchase Flow (Server):</strong> When a customer purchases a gift card, the backend orchestrates several steps atomically:</p>
<ol data-start="11624" data-end="14496">
<li data-start="11624" data-end="12853">
<p data-start="11627" data-end="12853"><strong data-start="11627" data-end="11661">Payment Processing via Square:</strong> The backend receives a payment nonce/token from the frontend (if using Square Web Payments SDK) and creates a payment charge via Square’s Payments API. In sandbox mode, this uses sandbox credentials; for production, it must use the live Square environment. <strong data-start="11919" data-end="11929">Check:</strong> The code should select the correct Square API base URL and access token based on environment (production vs sandbox)<span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=Each%20application%20you%20create%20in,are%20generally%20used%20for%20testing" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=Each%20application%20you%20create%20in,are%20generally%20used%20for%20testing" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span><span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/general-considerations/using-rest-api#:~:text=,path%20after%20the%20host%20name" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/general-considerations/using-rest-api#:~:text=,path%20after%20the%20host%20name" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span>. For example, Square’s SDK or API calls should target <code data-start="12175" data-end="12208">https://connect.squareup.com/v2</code> in live mode instead of the sandbox URL<span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/general-considerations/using-rest-api#:~:text=,path%20after%20the%20host%20name" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/general-considerations/using-rest-api#:~:text=,path%20after%20the%20host%20name" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span>. Using the wrong token or URL will cause authentication errors<span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=Using%20the%20wrong%20access%20token,error%20code" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=Using%20the%20wrong%20access%20token,error%20code" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span>. <strong data-start="12391" data-end="12406">Fix Prompt:</strong> <em data-start="12407" data-end="12774">Review the Square API client initialization in the backend. Use an env flag or separate env variables for sandbox vs production keys. For instance, <code data-start="12556" data-end="12577">SQUARE_ACCESS_TOKEN</code> and <code data-start="12582" data-end="12604">SQUARE_SANDBOX_TOKEN</code>, and choose the appropriate one depending on <code data-start="12650" data-end="12660">NODE_ENV</code>. Likewise, ensure the Square environment (perhaps a config in their SDK) is set to <code data-start="12744" data-end="12756">Production</code> for live deploy.</em><span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=,in%20the%20following%20cURL%20request" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=,in%20the%20following%20cURL%20request" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span><span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=,in%20the%20following%20cURL%20request" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=,in%20the%20following%20cURL%20request" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span></p>
</li>
<li data-start="12856" data-end="14204">
<p data-start="12859" data-end="14204"><strong data-start="12859" data-end="12882">Gift Card Creation:</strong> After a successful payment, the backend generates a gift card record. In the current implementation, this likely involves creating a unique gift code (and storing details like amount, sender, recipient email, message, and an initial status “active/unredeemed”). <strong data-start="13145" data-end="13155">Check:</strong> Code generation should be sufficiently random to prevent guessing or fraud. If codes are 8-10 characters, increase to a longer length or include a random UUID portion. Predictable codes are a risk – they must not be sequential or easily enumerable. Use a cryptographic random generator for codes. <strong data-start="13453" data-end="13468">Fix Prompt:</strong> <em data-start="13469" data-end="13702">Update gift card code generation to use a secure random method. For example, use Node’s <code data-start="13558" data-end="13578">crypto.randomBytes</code> to create a 128-bit value and encode as a hex string, or a UUID library, ensuring the code cannot be guessed by attackers.</em> Additionally, <strong data-start="13717" data-end="13747">enforce an idempotency key</strong> when creating the payment or gift card record<span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/general-considerations/using-rest-api#:~:text=Idempotency%20works%20as%20follows%3A" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/general-considerations/using-rest-api#:~:text=Idempotency%20works%20as%20follows%3A" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span>. Square’s Payments API allows an <code data-start="13866" data-end="13883">idempotency_key</code> to avoid double-charging if a request is retried<span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/general-considerations/using-rest-api#:~:text=Idempotency%20works%20as%20follows%3A" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/general-considerations/using-rest-api#:~:text=Idempotency%20works%20as%20follows%3A" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span>. The backend should generate a unique key per purchase request (perhaps use the gift card ID or order ID) and include it in the Square charge call. This prevents accidental duplicate charges on network retries or user double-clicks.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="14207" data-end="14496">
<p data-start="14210" data-end="14496"><strong data-start="14210" data-end="14235">Email/PDF Generation:</strong> Once the gift card is created, the backend generates the <strong data-start="14293" data-end="14312">PDF certificate</strong> and <strong data-start="14317" data-end="14328">QR code</strong>, then sends an email. (These services are addressed separately below.) The purchase endpoint should handle errors carefully at this stage – see “Error Handling” below.</p>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li data-start="14498" data-end="16653">
<p data-start="14500" data-end="14706">[❌] <strong data-start="14504" data-end="14543">Gift Card Redemption Flow (Server):</strong> The backend must allow a merchant to redeem a gift card, marking it as used so it cannot be reused fraudulently. <strong data-start="14657" data-end="14667">Check:</strong> The redemption endpoint should verify:</p>
<ul data-start="14709" data-end="14971">
<li data-start="14709" data-end="14760">
<p data-start="14711" data-end="14760">The authenticity of the request (merchant’s JWT).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="14763" data-end="14879">
<p data-start="14765" data-end="14879">The gift card code exists, belongs to that merchant (if each merchant’s codes are distinct) or is globally unique.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="14882" data-end="14968">
<p data-start="14884" data-end="14968">The card is still valid (not already redeemed, not expired if an expiration is set).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="14974" data-end="16194"><strong data-start="14974" data-end="14993">Current status:</strong> It’s unclear if a redemption route is fully implemented. If not, this is critical to add. <strong data-start="15084" data-end="15099">Fix Prompt:</strong> <em data-start="15100" data-end="15245">Implement <code data-start="15111" data-end="15129">POST /api/redeem</code> (or similar): Accept a gift card code (and perhaps merchant ID from token), look up the gift card in the database.</em> If found, and <code data-start="15260" data-end="15277">redeemed==false</code>, mark it as redeemed (and possibly record the date/time and which user redeemed it). If not found or already redeemed, return an error. This logic must be <strong data-start="15433" data-end="15443">atomic</strong> to avoid race conditions (e.g. two redemption requests at the same time for the same code – ensure only one succeeds by checking and updating in a single DB transaction if possible). Additionally, <strong data-start="15641" data-end="15665">authorization check:</strong> the merchant redeeming should only be allowed to redeem gift cards that belong to <em data-start="15748" data-end="15755">their</em> store. For example, if gift cards are tagged with a <code data-start="15808" data-end="15820">merchantId</code>, compare it with <code data-start="15838" data-end="15851">req.user.id</code> from the JWT. Reject the request if they don’t match (to prevent one merchant redeeming another’s card). <strong data-start="15957" data-end="15970">Response:</strong> On success, return a clear response (perhaps the remaining balance, which would be 0 after full redemption, or just a success message). The front-end will use this to confirm to the merchant user that the card is redeemed.</p>
<p data-start="16198" data-end="16653">If the project intended to integrate with Square’s Gift Card API for redemption (i.e. using Square’s <strong data-start="16299" data-end="16313">Gift Cards</strong> and <strong data-start="16318" data-end="16342">Gift Card Activities</strong> APIs), then the backend’s redemption may instead involve calling Square to redeem. In that case, similar checks apply plus Square’s confirmation. However, given the complexity (and likely lack of multi-merchant OAuth in this phase), it’s more probable the system is using its own redemption logic as described.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="16655" data-end="19365">
<p data-start="16657" data-end="16777">[✔️] <strong data-start="16662" data-end="16704">Square API Integration (Test vs Live):</strong> The code handles Square API calls, but confirm it toggles appropriately:</p>
<ul data-start="16780" data-end="19365">
<li data-start="16780" data-end="17351">
<p data-start="16782" data-end="17351"><strong data-start="16782" data-end="16800">Access Tokens:</strong> Square provides separate sandbox and production access tokens for each app<span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=Each%20application%20you%20create%20in,are%20generally%20used%20for%20testing" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=Each%20application%20you%20create%20in,are%20generally%20used%20for%20testing" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span>. Verify that <strong data-start="16928" data-end="16942">production</strong> tokens (from the Square Developer Dashboard) are configured via env vars for deployment, and that sandbox tokens are not accidentally used in live mode. The base API URL should switch from <code data-start="17132" data-end="17161">connect.squareupsandbox.com</code> (test) to <code data-start="17172" data-end="17194">connect.squareup.com</code> (production)<span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/general-considerations/using-rest-api#:~:text=,path%20after%20the%20host%20name" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/general-considerations/using-rest-api#:~:text=,path%20after%20the%20host%20name" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span>, as noted above. Mistakes here will cause authentication errors<span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=Using%20the%20wrong%20access%20token,error%20code" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=Using%20the%20wrong%20access%20token,error%20code" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="17354" data-end="18501">
<p data-start="17356" data-end="18501"><strong data-start="17356" data-end="17380">Square Webhook URLs:</strong> If the backend is set up to receive Square webhooks (for example, Square can send a payment update or a gift card event via webhook), ensure that in the Square Developer Portal the <strong data-start="17562" data-end="17590">Webhook Subscription URL</strong> is updated to the production URL of your app. For instance, if in test you used a tool like ngrok or a Replit URL, those need to be replaced with the real domain in the Square dashboard. <strong data-start="17778" data-end="17793">Fix Prompt:</strong> <em data-start="17794" data-end="17837">Configure Square webhooks for production:</em> in the Square dashboard, add your production endpoint (e.g. <code data-start="17898" data-end="17940">https://&lt;your-domain&gt;/api/square-webhook</code>) for relevant events (payments, gift card activities, etc.). Also, in code, verify the webhook handling route is secured (Square signs webhooks or provides a signature header – consider verifying it to ensure authenticity). If no webhook handling is implemented but is needed for full sync (e.g. to listen for gift card redemption outside the app), implement it now. Otherwise, if not using webhooks, remove any obsolete webhook code references and be prepared to handle Square’s automatic retries for webhooks by responding with 200 OK as quickly as possible.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="18504" data-end="18949">
<p data-start="18506" data-end="18949"><strong data-start="18506" data-end="18535">Square Environment Flags:</strong> It can be helpful to have a single configuration flag, e.g. <code data-start="18596" data-end="18623">SQUARE_ENV = 'production'</code> or <code data-start="18627" data-end="18646">USE_SANDBOX=false</code>, to flip the environment. Ensure that all Square SDK initializations respect this flag. (For example, in Square’s Node SDK, you initialize the client with an environment setting; double-check this is correctly set for live<span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=Using%20access%20tokens%20with%20Square,SDKs" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=Using%20access%20tokens%20with%20Square,SDKs" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span><span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]"><a href="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=%24client%20%3D%20new%20SquareClient,value%20%5D" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://developer.squareup.com/docs/build-basics/access-tokens#:~:text=%24client%20%3D%20new%20SquareClient,value%20%5D" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-full grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">developer.squareup.com</span></span></span></a></span></span>.)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="18952" data-end="19365">
<p data-start="18954" data-end="19365"><strong data-start="18954" data-end="18985">Testing in Sandbox vs Live:</strong> As a final pre-live step, run a full purchase flow in the Square <strong data-start="19051" data-end="19062">Sandbox</strong> environment to ensure the integration works (Square sandbox requires special test card numbers and returns dummy transactions). Then do a small test in production with a real transaction (perhaps with a $1 charge) to verify end-to-end behavior with real payments, <strong data-start="19327" data-end="19337">before</strong> announcing the system live.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="19367" data-end="20955">
<p data-start="19369" data-end="19578">[❌] <strong data-start="19373" data-end="19400">PDF Generation Service:</strong> The backend generates a PDF gift card (presumably containing the gift card code, QR code, merchant name, message, and perhaps branding). <strong data-start="19538" data-end="19557">Live readiness:</strong> Check the following:</p>
<ul data-start="19581" data-end="20508">
<li data-start="19581" data-end="19814">
<p data-start="19583" data-end="19814"><strong data-start="19583" data-end="19604">Content Accuracy:</strong> Verify the PDF template uses the correct details (especially any monetary amount, code, and recipient name). In test mode, sample data might have been used – ensure in production it uses actual purchase data.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="19817" data-end="20004">
<p data-start="19819" data-end="20004"><strong data-start="19819" data-end="19843">Branding and Polish:</strong> If the PDF is customer-facing, ensure logos or headers are correct for production (no “Test” watermark or placeholder logo). Remove any debug info from the PDF.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="20007" data-end="20156">
<p data-start="20009" data-end="20156"><strong data-start="20009" data-end="20030">File Size/Format:</strong> Test the PDF on multiple PDF readers to ensure it opens. Optimize the PDF file size if possible (large images can bloat it).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="20159" data-end="20505">
<p data-start="20161" data-end="20505"><strong data-start="20161" data-end="20183">Generation Errors:</strong> If PDF generation fails (e.g. library throws an error), handle it gracefully: log the error and ensure the system can still send at least a text email with the code as a fallback. You might consider queuing a retry for PDF generation if a transient error occurs (though PDF generation errors are rare beyond coding bugs).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="20511" data-end="20589"><strong data-start="20511" data-end="20526">Fix Prompt:</strong> <em data-start="20527" data-end="20576">Implement error handling around PDF generation.</em> For example:</p>

</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="20783" data-end="20955">Possibly notify an admin if a PDF fails in production. Ensure the PDF filename or content doesn’t expose any internal path (use a generic name like <code data-start="20931" data-end="20952">GiftCard_&lt;code&gt;.pdf</code>).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="20957" data-end="22501">
<p data-start="20959" data-end="21132">[❌] <strong data-start="20963" data-end="20986">QR Code Generation:</strong> The QR code representing the gift card is likely generated using a library (e.g. generating a data URI image or an SVG/PDF embedding). <strong data-start="21122" data-end="21132">Check:</strong></p>
<ul data-start="21135" data-end="22095">
<li data-start="21135" data-end="21477">
<p data-start="21137" data-end="21477"><strong data-start="21137" data-end="21154">Data Encoded:</strong> Determine if the QR encodes a URL or just the raw gift card code. If it’s a URL (for example <code data-start="21248" data-end="21288">https://yourapp.com/redeem?code=ABC123</code>), make sure it uses the <strong data-start="21313" data-end="21334">production domain</strong> in live mode. Hardcoding a localhost or dev URL in QR would be a live bug. Use an environment variable for the base URL if constructing links.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="21480" data-end="21736">
<p data-start="21482" data-end="21736"><strong data-start="21482" data-end="21504">Scanning Workflow:</strong> The system assumes a merchant or user can scan this QR. Test scanning the produced QR with a smartphone: does it correctly open the redemption page or present the code? In a controlled environment, simulate the end user experience.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="21739" data-end="22092">
<p data-start="21741" data-end="22092"><strong data-start="21741" data-end="21754">Security:</strong> If the QR code URL (if used) allows automatic redemption, be careful – it’s better if it simply pre-fills the code and still requires the merchant to confirm (so that a lost printed gift card isn’t redeemed by just anyone scanning it). It sounds like currently the QR is likely just a convenience to avoid typing the code, which is good.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="22098" data-end="22161"><strong data-start="22098" data-end="22113">Fix Prompt:</strong> <em data-start="22114" data-end="22154">Update QR code content for production:</em> e.g.,</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible!" data-start="22164" data-end="22248"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center
